## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 79 page(s) - 79 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a aria-current="page" class="" href="/">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://cloudscape.design/
- https://cloudscape.design/foundation/core-principles/accessibility/
- https://cloudscape.design/foundation/core-principles/accessibility/Building-accessible-experiences/
- https://cloudscape.design/foundation/core-principles/accessibility/focus-management-principles/
- https://cloudscape.design/about/
- *...and 74 more page(s)*

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://cloudscape.design/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a aria-current="page" class="" href="/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="awsui_button_vjswe_1mmk1_157 awsui_variant-primary_vjswe_1mmk1_235 awsui_link_vjswe_1mmk1_654" data-analytics-funnel-value="button:R65jralefkq:" href="/get-started/" style="padding-block:5.5px;padding-inline:20px">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="awsui_button_vjswe_1mmk1_157 awsui_variant-primary_vjswe_1mmk1_235 awsui_link_vjswe_1mmk1_654"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="awsui_button_vjswe_1mmk1_157 awsui_variant-normal_vjswe_1mmk1_206 awsui_link_vjswe_1mmk1_654" data-analytics-funnel-value="button:Ra5jralefkq:" href="/demos/" style="padding-block:5.5px;padding-inline:20px">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="awsui_button_vjswe_1mmk1_157 awsui_variant-normal_vjswe_1mmk1_206 awsui_link_vjswe_1mmk1_654"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a id="link-self:RjblpqjralefkqH1:" class="awsui_link_4c84z_1i0rz_145 awsui_variant-primary_4c84z_1i0rz_247 awsui_font-size-heading-m_4c84z_1i0rz_497" data-analytics-funnel-value="link:Rjblpqjralefkq:" href="/foundation/">Foundation</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@id="link-self:RjblpqjralefkqH1:"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a id="link-self:RlblpqjralefkqH1:" class="awsui_link_4c84z_1i0rz_145 awsui_variant-primary_4c84z_1i0rz_247 awsui_font-size-heading-m_4c84z_1i0rz_497" data-analytics-funnel-value="link:Rlblpqjralefkq:" href="/components/">Components</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@id="link-self:RlblpqjralefkqH1:"]`

*... and 11 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.07:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

### https://cloudscape.design/foundation/core-principles/accessibility/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a aria-current="page" class="" href="/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a aria-current="page" class="website-navigation-link-active" href="/foundation/">Foundation</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="website-navigation-link-active"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="awsui_anchor_1kosq_1v1qx_159" href="/" tabindex="0">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="awsui_anchor_1kosq_1v1qx_159"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<span class="awsui_anchor_1kosq_1v1qx_159" aria-current="page" aria-disabled="true" tabindex="0" role="link">...</span>`
- XPath: `/span[@class="awsui_anchor_1kosq_1v1qx_159"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="awsui_anchor-link_swimc_d8hyd_281 awsui_anchor-link_17oho_5eh15_17" href="#accessibility-in-cloudscape">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="awsui_anchor-link_swimc_d8hyd_281 awsui_anchor-link_17oho_5eh15_17"]`

*... and 7 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button aria-label="Mark page as helpful" title="Mark page as helpful" class="awsui_button_vjswe_1mmk1_157 awsui_variant-normal_vjswe_1mmk1_206" data-analytics-funnel-value="button:Rddqjtrajalefkq:" type="submit">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="awsui_button_vjswe_1mmk1_157 awsui_variant-normal_vjswe_1mmk1_206"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a aria-current="page" class="" href="/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a aria-current="page" class="website-navigation-link-active" href="/patterns/">Patterns</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="website-navigation-link-active"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="awsui_anchor_1kosq_1v1qx_159" href="/" tabindex="0">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="awsui_anchor_1kosq_1v1qx_159"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<span class="awsui_anchor_1kosq_1v1qx_159" aria-current="page" aria-disabled="true" tabindex="0" role="link">...</span>`
- XPath: `/span[@class="awsui_anchor_1kosq_1v1qx_159"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="awsui_anchor-link_swimc_d8hyd_281 awsui_anchor-link_17oho_5eh15_17" href="#key-ux-concepts">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="awsui_anchor-link_swimc_d8hyd_281 awsui_anchor-link_17oho_5eh15_17"]`

*... and 11 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button aria-label="Mark page as helpful" title="Mark page as helpful" class="awsui_button_vjswe_1mmk1_157 awsui_variant-normal_vjswe_1mmk1_206" data-analytics-funnel-value="button:Rddqjtrajalefkq:" type="submit">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="awsui_button_vjswe_1mmk1_157 awsui_variant-normal_vjswe_1mmk1_206"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<h3 id="corresponding-with-breadcrumbs-optional" class="awsui_root_18wu0_114z2_934 awsui_box_18wu0_114z2_172 awsui_h3-variant_18wu0_114z2_176 awsui_color-default_18wu0_114z2_172 awsui_font-size-default_18wu0_114z2_188 awsui_font-weight-default_18wu0_114z2_228">Corresponding with breadcrumbs - optional</h3>`
- XPath: `/h3[@id="corresponding-with-breadcrumbs-optional"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<h3 id="corresponding-with-breadcrumbs" class="awsui_root_18wu0_114z2_934 awsui_box_18wu0_114z2_172 awsui_h3-variant_18wu0_114z2_176 awsui_color-default_18wu0_114z2_172 awsui_font-size-default_18wu0_114z2_188 awsui_font-weight-default_18wu0_114z2_228">Corresponding with breadcrumbs</h3>`
- XPath: `/h3[@id="corresponding-with-breadcrumbs"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R53: Headings follow a logical hierarchy](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h4 class="awsui_root_18wu0_114z2_934 awsui_box_18wu0_114z2_172 awsui_h4-variant_18wu0_114z2_176 awsui_m-top-xxs_18wu0_114z2_718 awsui_color-default_18wu0_114z2_172 awsui_font-size-default_18wu0_114z2_188 awsui_font-weight-default_18wu0_114z2_228">...</h4>`
- XPath: `/h4[@class="awsui_root_18wu0_114z2_934 awsui_box_18wu0_114z2_172 awsui_h4-variant_18wu0_114z2_176 awsui_m-top-xxs_18wu0_114z2_718 awsui_color-default_18wu0_114z2_172 awsui_font-size-default_18wu0_114z2_188 awsui_font-weight-default_18wu0_114z2_228"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.07:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="awsui_description_2qdw9_hjb9x_348 awsui_description-variant-h1_2qdw9_hjb9x_355 awsui_refresh_2qdw9_hjb9x_221">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="awsui_description_2qdw9_hjb9x_348 awsui_description-variant-h1_2qdw9_hjb9x_355 awsui_refresh_2qdw9_hjb9x_221"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="awsui_description_2qdw9_hjb9x_348 awsui_description-variant-h1_2qdw9_hjb9x_355 awsui_refresh_2qdw9_hjb9x_221">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="awsui_description_2qdw9_hjb9x_348 awsui_description-variant-h1_2qdw9_hjb9x_355 awsui_refresh_2qdw9_hjb9x_221"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R80: ASCII art has a text alternative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r80)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="awsui_description_2qdw9_hjb9x_348 awsui_description-variant-h1_2qdw9_hjb9x_355 awsui_refresh_2qdw9_hjb9x_221">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="awsui_description_2qdw9_hjb9x_348 awsui_description-variant-h1_2qdw9_hjb9x_355 awsui_refresh_2qdw9_hjb9x_221"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

### https://cloudscape.design/components/avatar/

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<footer class="pagefooter ignore-by-llm-markdown" role="navigation" aria-label="footer">`
- XPath: `footer`
